# Crafting implementation status

Target game version: **0.5.4**. Canonical machine-readable detail: `reports/crafting-implementation-status.json`.

“Implemented” in the tables means source-backed `verified`; `inferred` mechanics are operational but remain explicitly labelled as inference. Every retained definition is classified—none is silently treated as available merely because it appears in the catalogue.

## Pre-implementation audit

This is the Phase 1 registry checkpoint captured before the Essence/socket mechanics slice:

|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|

| Socketing / Augments | 296 | 0 | 0 | 288 | 8 | 0 |

Current catalogue-only categories (zero verified or inferred operations): Quality, Delirium / Instilling, Runeforging, Corruption / Sacrifice.

No individual definition remains in the unexplained `catalogue_only` state. Discoverable definitions without mechanics are classified as `blocked`, `deprecated`, or `non_equipment` and carry an exact question.

## Audit findings

Existing supported UI handlers:

- `executeCraftOperation -> applyAlchemy`: 1
- `executeCraftOperation -> applyAnnulment`: 1
- `executeCraftOperation -> applyArtificerOrb`: 1
- `executeCraftOperation -> applyAugmentation`: 3
- `executeCraftOperation -> applyChaos`: 3
- `executeCraftOperation -> applyDivine`: 1
- `executeCraftOperation -> applyEssence`: 81
- `executeCraftOperation -> applyEssenceOfAbyss`: 1
- `executeCraftOperation -> applyExalted`: 3
- `executeCraftOperation -> applyFracturing`: 1
- `executeCraftOperation -> applyHinekoraLock`: 1
- `executeCraftOperation -> applyRegal`: 3
- `executeCraftOperation -> applySocketable`: 284
- `executeCraftOperation -> applyTransmutation`: 3
- `executeCraftOperation -> startDesecrationFlow`: 7
- `executeCraftOperation -> toggleCraftOmen`: 14
- `executeCraftOperation -> toggleOmen`: 4

Discoverable but disabled definitions:

- Currency: 0
- Quality: 8
- Socketing / Augments: 3
- Ritual / Omens: 19
- Essences: 0
- Abyss: 4
- Breach / Genesis: 27
- Delirium / Instilling: 26
- Runeforging: 17
- Corruption / Sacrifice: 3

Mechanics implemented directly from checked-in retained data:

- 80 regular, Greater, and Perfect Essence definitions with exact normalized class-to-modifier mappings
- Essence of the Breach with its retained Amulet/Ring forced prefix identity
- Artificer's Orb using the retained concrete-base socket count as an explicitly inferred cap
- 287 non-deprecated Runes, Soul Cores, Idols, Abyssal Eyes, and Congealed Mist records with exact retained effects and limit codes

Mechanics implemented from the supplied PoE2DB files: none. Those files were used for route and schema research only; see `reports/poe2db-data-sources.md`.

Genuinely ambiguous mechanics remain blocked. Their full blocker and exact unresolved question appear in the per-definition tables and JSON report.
